Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	In this method, you make three or four cauteries, aligning them along the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cauteries we have mentioned before; and do not press your hand on the entire cauterization, and let the hairs be close by its back; and another method of cauterization is that you heat the cauterization that has two needles, as we have shown in the shoulder dislocation; and lift the curvature that is near the mouse's ear, or where the pain from the ear comes from the left side, and let the elevations that you lift the curvature according to its curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterization should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After you have bound the two nerves, burn them until the keeper is perceived from the other side, and then remove the cautery, and thus you will have four. And if you see, then cauterize the entire cautery at three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has gotten pus from long tension, and this is worth mentioning as another cure before mentioned.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterizing is not good for hydropsy, except in the manner which is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cautery around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the kidneys, and one behind the back above the spine, and one at the worst place; and let the cauteries be close to the edge of the keeper.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the cauterizer open for a long time to stop bleeding, and not neglecting the care of the wound after the cauterization; and healing would be hastened, and together with the help of God, the two intentions would be achieved.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cauterizer for the stomach is like the one we have shown before; and for the back, it is olive-shaped, as it is written above.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the inflammation of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are inflamed in one who is hydroptic, and are plain of yellow bile, you must cauterize above the foot between the auricular and annular; and relieve your hand with the cauterizer towards returning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply into the flesh, thus avoiding the yellowish part, and let the cautery be done in this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After applying two cautery irons on each leg at the tip of the spatula; and let the cautery be long, one behind the knee in front and the other in front of the knee on the leg; and leave the cautery over a longer period to cure the wound that has been made.
de la menoison	of the misalignment
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the solution of the stomach comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues that are in the stomach and in the intestines are obstructed, and cannot be cured by other means of treatment; and you see the pain is very severe and of great benefit, then apply a large cautery over the stomach according to what has been said before about the cautery of the stomach, with the cautery circulating; and four cautery irons around the belly, all the thin cautery clamps, and two cautery irons on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering from pain, apply fire cauterization on the nipple, and I cauterization on each island, and II small cauterizations on the stomach below the large one, for the cure is beneficial when it has good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of worms
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the worms are deeply rooted, or one or more, and are ancient and are large humors cold and moist corroded, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not benefit, then apply fire cauterization: III on the spine of the back, which is entirely before unmelted little by little in triangular, and I cauterization outside the belly II doses; and if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the food does not cook, and one sees the face swells, then the face apply I large cauterization on the stomach, as it is previously said, and I other on the liver, and I other on the mouse at all the cauterization clavile; and leave the cauterization open long tense.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, the patient as long as they are healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the skin disease called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you apply the cautery, if it seems like a razor, and then put it all on fire above the "thelul" spot; and let your hand be as long as the cauterizer comes near the base of the vein, from which the blood flows; do this once or twice, and if there is much "thelul", cauterize each one as we have said; after curing the wounds as long as they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a large cautery above the "thelul", it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wounds cannot be suffered by a surgeon or opened, as we will tell you about in its place, then comes illness that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any comes fistula, and is awake and given porridge and corrupted moisture, then you must provide the whole tent with a thin skin, and guard that you clean the tent as much as it has of purity.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cauterizer which seems like a razor, and putting it into the fistula according to the quantity that the tent has entered, and start the cauterization as long as those cors are burned and corrupted, once, or two, or three, according to the quantity of the wound; and guard against burning the nerves which are inside, and the great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and the intestine, you should avoid these areas, and only do so in the area that is not too thin, and think that it is not healed; after healing the area as long as it is healthy, and if the area is still sore, and the matter is removed along with the tension, then wash the area that is completely healed; and if the matter is not removed, and the area is still sore, and the bone is corrupted at the source, and thus like one of those that we will say in its area.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain of the flank comes to the kidneys, and with great swelling, and does not take the form of a woman, then it is necessary that you do fire cautery on the kidneys from both sides at the clavile cautery that we have previously mentioned; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and they will be greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is small and weak from dryness and moisture, if the hairs retain urine, then cauterize in the part before the bladder, where the hairs begin to grow, on the right and on the left, and let each cautery be as long as a needle; and do one cauterization in front of the back, or two if you have need; and let the clavile cauteries be done according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marsh is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms late; and when they come, they cause great pain: therefore it is necessary to do three cautery around the womb, as we have said about cauterization of the bladder, and two cauterizations in front of the back; and let the clavile cauteries be done as we have said.
de la hainche	of the waist
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When viscous moisture descends to the waist bone, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the legs are found to be bent, then you must cauterize the pain above the waist bone with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign before the bone around the waist so that it returns, so that the waist is inside the circle; and if it is such a cautery as has been cauterized in the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this cauterization is not present, then make three cauterizations of large olive-sized ones, and let the cauterizations be as before for all the curatives; and the cure until they are healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is from cold and moisture, and the hairs are cured of what we have said in the division and the cure does not work, and the disease is ancient: therefore it is necessary that you purge the hairs of the large humors with bad-smelling pills, or other good-smelling pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the fire cauterization; and the manner of this cauterization is according to two methods: that is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cauterization is according to many methods, of which some are: that you cauterize above the hip joint three triangular cauterizations in this form, and do good depth and great, and let there be between each cauterization a space of an inch, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped; never made on the middle above the hip, because it is there four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that the cauterizer uses the circular instrument that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the shoulder; but do it in a different way so that the circle contains the entire shoulder and all the tendons should be included.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the shoulder and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes to the thigh and leg, then make two cautery marks where the pain is located, and one cautery mark above the ankle four fingers wide, on the right side a little; and let the cauterizing instrument be sharp, and let the thickness of the tendon be included; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two or three fingers or near the foot, then cauterize where he feels the pain three times or four with the cautery mark called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it is a job, do more; and if the pain is from the groin to the thigh, apply cauterization with a cutaneous or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I myself have seen many who applied cauterization above the ankle of the foot, and burned so much that the leg was completely deformed, and the feet also, and all the bones were perforated and rotten.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a vomiting spell from which they died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, perform cauterization in one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise say in the cauterization of the back, because of this method, use such a sharp and as large as a navillon of a finger, or a little less, and it should be inserted between the ribs and inserted from one to the other at a distance equal to the thickness of a thumb; and the inserts should be above two parts, and they should also be like needles, and there is a good handle of iron. And this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And it should be heated until it is all red and the senses are gone, and then place it on the back of the painful back, and turn it over to the healthy side; and the cauterization once with the cauterizer and leave it for three days; and then apply a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for ten days; after the ointment cure until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little due to its frightful appearance, and few see those who use it; nevertheless, it is a good cauterizer, which can bear the heat, and where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cauterizing instruments of medicine are such that you make them into a punch with an edge on the margin of the door, and either of brass or iron at one end, and in the height have II, and between each has the quantity of the size of a pin; and they are open below and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing the board of the back on the painful side lying down, and quickly applying your hand over the board of the back; afterwards pour between the two circles of the hot water which has been heated at the fire one pint, and let it stand for an hour, and suffer the pain with the heat and the burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is true that the burning is as painful as fire; and when the burning has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the back gently, and let it rest for three hours, and put butter on it until the black scorching is removed; and let it rest for three hours so that the purity is restored; and this would be the last aid after the cure of wounds as long as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, use the instrument that you have made for the abdomen, according to what you have done in the abdomen, and this is the method of the hot bath, and I have written it where I treat the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take equal amounts of quicklime and fresh charcoal, grind them together, and put them in a new earthenware pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Or if there is a small hole where the point of a razor cannot enter; and put that pot in another well-closed pot, and put over it alkali and charcoal and hot water until there are two above the powders, so that you will have it well prepared in your hand; and let it remain until all the water has dripped off or the pot is broken, then take all the water and pour it over the charcoal and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And if it is very painful and administered in the form of medical operations and cauterization of other members, because it does its work like fire, and if it is used with other medicines that are well cauterized on the back, such as anacardium and chalk mixed with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galen tells us of a cure that some were cured of the pain in the back and sciatic vein, and they were very happy, and he says that no other cure was given, and that they were cured once when this cure was given, and he was bathed as he teaches here afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And in a similar manner, you should apply a fresh, green willow bark, and grind it thoroughly with a little grease, and put on the back and thighs and legs where the pain is, and bind it; and let it stay for three hours, and by the amount that the pains do not feel the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then let him enter a warm bath as much as the body is slightly warmed, and make him lie down, and the pain will go away and be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And let it be known that no one should use such cauterizing medicines unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Hippocrates said that when the vein is cut, it should be cauterized with iron from sheep, and this helps much; and the cautery should be made in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another and the old oil, and pour it into the fossa between the thumb and the other one called foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Then take some dry sheep fat, and put it in the fire until it becomes charcoal, and pour it onto the cloth, and leave it until it is soaked; and do this again, and do not stop doing this until you think by sense that it comes close to the back, and that the pain has ceased; and this method of cauterization is called "cautere de chievre".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of two bones
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or from impact or from too much bloodletting, or from similar expansive cold matter, none of these is as effective as cauterization, because it comes from the heat of hot matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary that after the pain has been emptied of fetid pills or similar things, which are placed on top of the back where the pain is, three lines thick with cauteries, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the power and quantity that the pain can bear; and let the cauteries be done according to the cauterizing iron called "poins"; and if you see, make III cauteries or IV at the average cauterizing iron of this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often comes to small children, and the signs of onset are that they have narrow aliment when walking, and fear; and you feel in the last spinous process of the back and in us the appearance that comes above the other spinous processes.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this disease and you want to cure it, if you cauterize with the fire cautery in this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery grips each part of the spinous process.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if you cauterize around the spinous process with the fire cautery gripping II lines or III, and the points are near each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment, the patient should be kept as healthy as possible according to what we have said, and you must not apply cauterization with a sharp instrument that is near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of the joints is due to moisture that has spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes suddenly, which is properly called "gout", and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this way: apply a great deal of cauterization around the joint, and the cauterizing oil should be applied in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a sign that you should hold the face of the child during the cauterization, then perform the entire cauterization with the claim "not here".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come from the jaw and other joints, and it happens often, then perform cauterization on each jaw with three or four cautery rods from each part, at the entire olive oil cauterization; and if you have more skill, do so, but do not hold your hand further than the tip of the curved rod of the healer.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the jaw and back, then administer the cauterization that we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are severe, apply points two lines apart; and if they remain unchanged, apply points above each joint and above the hair of the hand; and if the pains come from the wrists or shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good government to the patient and proper medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good government and purge the humor, he will be healed by the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the gaping wound
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the gaping wound comes in anger, and the bowels descend into the abdomen and this is new, it is necessary that when you see to cure him, that he not move much that day; and that you use things that reduce the belly, so that the contents of his belly do not fall out; afterwards make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his breath until the bowels are returned, and pull them back with your fingers, and press down on the wound above the bone of the thumb, and at all signs that resemble a half-circle above the body; then heat the cautery with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and drips senselessly.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the mud from its place; and the attendants stain their hands above so they do not return backward; and work well on the thighs with the hairs, and put some oil on him on the knees and on the joints, and the other on the worst that stains his hands; then put the cauterizer on all of your hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again with another one until you come close to the bone; and be careful that the mud does not escape when you do the cauterizer; that you do not burn it; and that by this way the pain does not kill, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And when you do not reach the bone with the fire cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cauterization of children should be subtle according to their age, and adults according to their size; after three days, care for the wound with butter until the burn is healed; then care for other injuries as long as they are healed, and let the hairs grow long on their back until the wound is well sealed; and it should be washed thoroughly, so that the pus does not spread when they move around.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to rise, give him a well-made bandage, and let it remain for forty more days; and let him have good rest, that he may work little and avoid too much repletion from drinking and eating, and too high elevation; and if he follows this instruction, he is entirely sound.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will tell you afterwards about the treatment of cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the renting of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When rents come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let one-third of the care be applied; after the cure according to what we have said; and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the cautery at three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first signify the shoulder joint and make a line for the width above the fracture, and another behind, and with your hand hold all the cauterizing iron.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	but the first cauteries are lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	when pain comes in any limb, whether it is to fall or to strike, and this pain lasts long, and the cure of medicine does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called «poins», and the cauteries should follow the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its strength and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cautery is healthy, it's good; if not, start another cautery above the first one, as it is customary that the wound should be made to the member that is nearest, because you must make the cauteries until the injuries are healed.
de meselerie	of medicine
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Medicine is never helped by cauterization with great help, and even the disease that comes from putrefaction of the humor and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you see cauterization, take care if the disease is at the beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not spread or remain, and you doubt that corruption may spread throughout the injury, then make these cauterizations: I on the forehead and the other towards the front at the end of the eyebrows; II above the two eyes, and I behind the temple; and leave as much hand as the cauterization comes just to the bone, and as long as the eschars come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape; and cauterize on the mouse according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the infection is widely spread; and it is clearly apparent, then it is necessary that you cauterize with these cauteries that we have said or chief, and the cautery at the base of the nose, and two cauteries above the spine of the neck, and six cauteries above the spine of the back, and one great one and one other below, and two above the shoulders, and two above the elbows, and two above the knees, and two above each joint of the hands and feet, and above the hand wounds; and beware of those that are above the buttocks calcifying, that you do not burn them; and never once make a cautery above the bone of the wrist, and one above the bone of the stomach, and one above the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And remember that the more you perform the cauterization, the less you should provide assistance, and it benefits him; and remember that the wounds do not feel pain as much as the healthy ones, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating the wound with flour and honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the swelling comes to any member and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healed, then perform cauterization on the member according to its size and smallness; and let the cauterization go a little into the skin; then treat the wounds until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And it is never done with fire cauterization by hand and at the wrist and at the back, at the end of the nerve that makes the limb move, and thus if it is swollen, it is stretched; and in no way does it interfere with anyone if they are not knowledgeable about the limbs and their movements.
de albaras	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	For the disease called "albaras" that is awakened, and medical means do not help, then cauterize with a cautery a little in advance, according to the quantity of the spice of choice, until the wound is healed, and its color is restored; then cure with flour of wheat and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and coltsfoot and alder, each part; and mix everything together, and bind it on the affected area, and apply to the limb as long as it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chancres by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre first appears and you want to stop its spread, cauterize it with the cauterizing iron that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And all the sages say that one should also make the cauterization in the middle of the chancre; and I do not think this is good, because I believe it should not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it happen once; and a more important thing is that it be cauterized all around, with the cauterizing iron that is called «circle», as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the puffed up who cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati", and it lingers on the brink of death due to the excess it causes or because of the age of the patient when they are elderly (that is, too old) and have little blood, or due to the tension; and you see it hastening towards death: then cauterize around with many small cauteries while pricking; afterwards leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through the entire cauterization, then heat the cauterization from where this is the form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the surface, and be such that the cauteries feel the pain in a similar manner to the course of the pus being alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until they are perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a small amount of a member, for it misaligns the members as if the dry reeds were doing so.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization together with fire, then heat the cauteries sharp and large, according to what is needed for the leg or the disease; afterwards cauterize all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Let it rest for three days, and then apply the cauterized leather over the wounds, suffering with oil until the scorched parts of fire are removed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of wounds, worms generate char.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy worms do not arise, it is good; but if not, then restart the cauterization over the remaining leather.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has never been cured by medicine in place of fire cauterization; but the fire cauterization is of greater help, and I have already given the cure of the medicine in the division: take it when you have the opportunity.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the thorns that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	often come to the feet by defilement, and a disease arises which is called "closed" according to our understanding, and is a great harm that becomes the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries for this disease are in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to say, fire cauterization, and water-hot cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is that you heat the cauterizer like a quill, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can penetrate the nail on all parts, and that it has thin margins; afterwards, put it all hot on top of the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it comes to the end of the nail; and leave it thus for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment of wild herbs ground with silk, and leave the ointment all night, and the nail will fall off and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the injured limb with a warm poultice until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by deflowering the wound, and often in hands and feet, then it is necessary to apply cauterization with very hot iron; and it is done in this way: take a needle of brass or iron, or a quill pen, and place it on the nail and the cuticle, that is, pricking the warts; and place the needle so that it surrounds everything, then put a drop of very hot water, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand in turning so that the edge of the needle comes to the root of the nail, and find the very hot water deep into the root; and suffer the pain of the hot water for an hour; then leave it like this, and it will all fall out at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Then do another, until you have examined all those in the heart, then treat the wounds that engender pus which causes char.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment of the trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone trembles from cold or shivering, or from a quarter fever or other, it is necessary that you make four cauteries or four on the spine of the back; one cautery between each spine; and one below the belly, and one above the stomach at the olive cautery; this will let them tremble, and hasten the recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled abscesses
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No times appear due to previous causes, such as swollen, pus-filled sores, which come from large, corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is appropriate when they appear, then one should perform a cauterization above each head of the pustule: a subtle cauterization with the tip of a burning twig, or from the root of aristolochia long, or with the lenticular cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no times should they be cauterized at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and they cannot grow further, but are broken down by the excess from which they come, and are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there is great bleeding from the cut artery at the wound that comes from the sides, or at the incision of the abscess, or in the cauterization of the member, and similar things; and it is a very painful thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And in any case, if it happens to anyone, you must quickly place your first finger on the wound of the vein, and press very hard until the bleeding is stopped from your first finger, and no more blood comes out; then put on the fire cauteries of olive oil many times, both small and large, until they are all red; then take I, or great or small according to the wound and the limb in which the artery is pierced, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your first finger, and keep the cautery there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the first one fails when you lift your second finger above the vein, and the cauterizer is extinguished, then quickly take the other cauterizers that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is stopped; and be careful that you do not burn the nerve that is next to it, and that no other harm comes over the wound; and make sure that when the artery is not cut, it cannot be stopped immediately when the artery is large, unless by one of the four ways we have said: or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by a very tight bandage, or by medicines placed on top that have power to stop bleeding; and let it be tied and strained.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers tight binding with cloth or metal objects on top, or similar things, does not profit unless they do not.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they have no remedy present, they should place their finger index over the wound of the vein as we have said, and tightly bind it until it is cauterized above the wound and above the vein; and they should not move it, but keep it cold often with cold water until the flesh is frozen and swollen and cauterized; and make inquiries about what they need for cautery and remedies.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of remedies for tails
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first book all diseases for which it is necessary to cauterize with fire, or with a burning medicine, and the symptoms and causes and instruments and forms of cauteries; and I will put this chapter about the lower jaw from the neck downwards, and I will go into this chapter by that same way so that one may find more easily what one wants.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of cauteries, and therefore it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	In the work of this chapter, there has often been bloodletting when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from such people who have become so with their disease that they die immediately because of the remedy they find for their disease, and because of the greatness of its evil; and these one must fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And of these, there are those who give you their meaning, and say: "Wait, I am sharp"; and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	You should not grant consent to those who come to you who have this manner, but place greater caution in your honor than in your desire, and do not rashly but wisely from that of which you are certain, and which you have taken and lost; and use prediction and indication in the treatment of your illnesses for the sake of converting health; and this will help you to gain good reputation, and glory, and memory for the long term.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords grant you good understanding and uprightness, and if you wish to breathe from the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have ordered you to examine this chapter by comparing it with other chapters on cauteries, as I have done from the beginning to the end, so that you may find it more easily what concerns you.
dou chief plein d’aigue	full of sharp
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	This disease often occurs in children at birth, and when the child's head is held too tightly; and sometimes it comes from a cause that is not known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	I have never seen this disease except in children, and all those that I have seen died; and because it seems to me that it is better to avoid such work in treating them.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child who was complaining of a sharp pain, and the head was swelling each day until it could no longer be supported; and he thought so much of the moisture that he died, and this moisture is assembled outside the bone above the symphysis, between the jaw and the bone; and if the swelling is between the jaw and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you should make a wide incision in the head; and let it be as long as II, so that the moisture flows out; and get the shape of the splint:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more extensive, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the joint is dislocated from the bone, and you see the signs that you see the commissures of the shoulder open on each part, and the sharp pain when you press it with your hand inside, and it does not return to you: then you must make three cuts in the shoulder in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After closing the wounds with bandages and powders, and put wine and oil, and leave it so for five days; then reset it, and treat the wound with bandages and counter-irritants, and keep the shoulder immobilized, and gradually apply moisture to the dry meat until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	Another method of incision is to look for the largest part of the abscess and the sharpest point of the lancet; as it is never in front, never behind, never on the right, and never on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Cut the part of the abscess that is open, and fill it with the point of the lancet, and make the incision according to what you can do; and be careful not to cover the artery; and if there is blood flow, the hairs may die from the outflow of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	I'm sorry, I don't understand
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it has a certain disease called "cataract" in the eyes or in the pupil, and the disease is ancient, and the medical cure does not help much, then the curative treatment is to cauterize with fire that covers the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, when you see that the hairs cover, it is necessary to make the painful part of the head; then rub the neck with a rough cloth until the arteries open, then hold the painful part against all the cloth; then look where the blood comes from, and the ears on both sides are after the ears, and they are not replaced; then sign the ears of the cure, then cover each side with a strip of two parts of agile cloth, until the cut reaches the bone, and it should be through the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, push the spatula away from the artery and cover it above, cutting as if you should through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, if blood spurts out continuously from above.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open when felt, then measure the amount of space between three fingers, then enlarge and cut into the bone; and as much blood as needed should be put out, perhaps a little more or less depending on what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains above the bone point, if the cloth that was applied does not come into contact, then close and bind the wound, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of emigrain
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old emigrain comes, and the catarrh is severe, due to the moisture of tears and the chills in the temples and ancient sweat and similar things, and it is treated by methods of healing medicine and nothing seems to help, then we must strain the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have related.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of their extraction is that the hairs of his temples are made to face the other way, and listen to the artery that opens in the temple, because it opens well by its beating, and it is not replaced sooner than in any men who are too cold; and if it is replaced, then strain the skin with some cloths, then rub the leather of some rough cloth, and heat the leather with boiling hot water until the artery clearly opens; then take the spatula of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	then shave the light skin gently until you reach the artery, then cut it at the top with pincers, and remove all the threads that are stuck to each part; and if the artery is thin, turn it back to the point of the needle, then cover that part according to the amount of the two chapters.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	for if it is not covered, it will not heal completely.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and draw out some blood from the sixth canthus to the third; and if the artery is large, it is necessary that you tie it in two turns of a strong silk thread, which does not allow any blood to come before the suppuration of the wound, and comes out of the blood; then cover the excess between the two threads in the same hour, and then, if you see, if you cauterize the wound with the cutting cautery up to the bone until the chapters are covered; and this is the best work, if the wounds do not have fever and he is of hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	Because the fire cautery is to finish the swellings: for it is of greater help to swellings.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For the extraction of arteries, it is necessary to fill the wound with old cotton and place bandages well made; and when they are removed, care should be taken with dry medicines that produce heat and bandages until they are healed; and if without bleeding from the artery as you have worked, you must quickly cover it with a cauterizer, or you fill the wound with vinegar and hold it in your hand so that the bleeding does not stop, and freeze the wound with cold water until it stops bleeding, and hold it tightly; and what is more difficult and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein of this cauterizer cutting from II parts, but the cuts should be well spaced to last longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When instruments are too tightly tied, they hold less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And there should be between the two knives a large space, and then when you have sealed the two wounds, and you place the hot iron above so that it comes to the bone, and copper the vein in two places; and they should be separated between the two wounds because it is not known how much of this cauterization will be needed; and this is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes are flowing down the veins that are above the skin of the forehead, and it does not improve with any medical treatment, and you see the face of the illness becoming twisted, and they feel as if they are trembling; and their hair is held and moist so much that the hairs of the pillows are stained, and the pillows are soiled, and burned by the heat of the tears, if there is a need for this treatment.
